	@fclose($fp);
}
if (!is_file('doc/website/download.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/website/download.html');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('doc/website/download.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/website/download.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/website/download.html') != '56543575bfee6d37ff2539b7015a6ffc767807ec') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/website/download.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/website/download.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/website/download.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/website/download.html') !== '56543575bfee6d37ff2539b7015a6ffc767807ec') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/website/download.html') !== 'e250e1508f4f9d07b894a8f6142830596126976c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/website/download.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/website/download.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/website/download.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/website/download.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/website/download.html') !== '56543575bfee6d37ff2539b7015a6ffc767807ec') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/website/download.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/website/examples.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/website/examples.html');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('doc/website/examples.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/website/examples.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/website/examples.html') != '58d6d22bfc17737a0d5873e61ab45b79851d895c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/website/examples.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/website/examples.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/website/examples.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/website/examples.html') !== '58d6d22bfc17737a0d5873e61ab45b79851d895c') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/website/examples.html') !== '140b0b1e594ba38da8b22846bc84fb6713948ac5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/website/examples.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/website/examples.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/website/examples.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/website/examples.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/website/examples.html') !== '58d6d22bfc17737a0d5873e61ab45b79851d895c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/website/examples.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/website/features.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/website/features.html');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('doc/website/features.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/website/features.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/website/features.html') != '59acba905a38da4560af2c0f355dedaad366dddf') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/website/features.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/website/features.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/website/features.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/website/features.html') !== '59acba905a38da4560af2c0f355dedaad366dddf') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/website/features.html') !== 'e283ec69db60518435f3b23fad66ba5aeb618dbc') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/website/features.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/website/features.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/website/features.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/website/features.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/website/features.html') !== '59acba905a38da4560af2c0f355dedaad366dddf') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/website/features.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/website/support.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/website/support.html');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('doc/website/support.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/website/support.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/website/support.html') != 'fdf8aca692b410951c938f01b931c1b40189268e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/website/support.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/website/support.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/website/support.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/website/support.html') !== 'fdf8aca692b410951c938f01b931c1b40189268e') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/website/support.html') !== '3aee39f5b08d0481e26b9e72ad17164f365cfbb1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/website/support.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/website/support.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/website/support.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/website/support.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/website/support.html') !== 'fdf8aca692b410951c938f01b931c1b40189268e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/website/support.html');
		}
	}
}

	}

	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'f753745118dcc2bf6278a8fd06c956eb00437f1f') {

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != '15c8886444e3bb62e5bd3388a2f5b9f590317036') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '15c8886444e3bb62e5bd3388a2f5b9f590317036') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'ed25148656aa4a6d708686b215b15feac3a9db7d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '15c8886444e3bb62e5bd3388a2f5b9f590317036') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') != '1ec8a1d841a3914d332e005792cd3b41050d1a0e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '1ec8a1d841a3914d332e005792cd3b41050d1a0e') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== 'f922b60d8cd4fac1318300715cf3d05029d28cbf') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '1ec8a1d841a3914d332e005792cd3b41050d1a0e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
		}
	}
}
